name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:studio 70
info:Stayed in September 2023
info:Solo travelers
info:1 Review
rating:5
posted:Posted September 13, 2023
msg:It has been almost 5 years since I last visited Beijing, due to the pandemic and travel restrictions. In the years before the pandemic I would often stay at the Opposite House as it was in a great location, offered something different and was very relaxing. Being a bit sentimental and in need of a relaxing weekend, when faced with a reason to visit Beijing, my heart overruled my head and I ignored the price of the rooms and booked two nights.

Walking in to the hotel it has slightly changed, the fantastic bar it had moving to where the reception used to be and a trendy Sichuan restaurant taking its place. The lobby is still stunning and immediately relaxes you into the feel of the hotel.

Previously when I last stayed ,the staff while very friendly and efficient, but could come across a bit aloof. There is a noticeable difference now, there is a warmer approach, very friendly and eager to help, but not in an intrusive way. Vincent at the desk was especially helpful and friendly, arranging for some parcels to couriered for me.

The rooms are still the same, which is great, large, comfortable, clean, minimal, with a great wide and deep bath. The free mini bar is well stocked and bed is large and comfortable.

The new bar is very good, a different feeling to the old bar, however the service is still efficient and friendly, the environment relaxing and the Gin Batch, gin and tonics are wonderful. 

Overall a great and relaxing experience and I want to go back as soon as I can afford the time and cost.

Jon

msg:Because I knew the hotel was about to close, I took the opportunity to stay in Beijing for three nights on business in May to experience this very famous hotel. The three-day stay was not perfect. The first day seemed very inconsistent, especially when the lights in the room went out without any warning at 11 o'clock in the evening. The staff explained that it was a misjudgment of the sensor. From the next day onwards, the miraculous sensor function never had an error again. The overall stay was very comfortable. The room was spacious and bright, with a green foliage in front of the floor-to-ceiling windows. The furniture in the room was sp**** and streamlined. The wooden washbasin and bathtub were very distinctive. I have to say that this hotel, which opened in 2008, was really at the forefront of fashion at the time. And after so many years, the facilities have been well maintained. I have tried hotel catering several times, but in general, the restaurants on the basement floor are still Michelin-starred, and the yellow croaker smells too fishy. The service is very good. The staff delivered my takeaway orders quickly, which is very good. It's a pity that the gym closes at 10 o'clock, it's too early. I really like the small gift of skin care products. Before leaving, I took the note on the desk as a souvenir.

msg:0. First of all: As an architect, I have also done hotel design. This time I came to the hotel mainly to fully experience the hotel design and atmosphere of the Opposite House. So I carefully learned about everything from the overall interior and exterior of the hotel to the facilities, equipment, business formats, supporting services and operation management. It took me a whole day. In addition, the hotel announced in April that it would be closed for transformation and new retail, so it was a farewell study. After a day, I was still moved by a lot. It can be regarded as a design with personal identity and characteristics of Wei Yanwu. Many details of the hotel are difficult to see in other domestic hotels, including the entire tonality. The interior accessories are very meticulous, including water cups and utensils. In general, I feel that I can come to a very commercial and international place in Beijing to rest comfortably, just like going home. Solid wood is warm, yoga is healthy, green and natural, and the details are well provided. Comprehensive, high-end and unique experience, also quite Beijing cultural characteristics, which shows Wei Gong's learning and love of Chinese culture; 
1. Facilities: As the Virgo of Master Wei Yanwu in domestic boutique designer hotels in 2008, the facilities are all top-notch, the texture of the door lock switch is very good, the toilet roca, the texture is very good, the pure solid wood double wash basin suspended in the air is also one of the few in China, the shower experience is great, the stone floor pineapple surface has a good anti-slip effect, I personally feel that the best facility should be the solid wood bathtub, soaking in it to experience full marks, the rest of the solid wood floor can be walked barefoot very comfortable, the indoor glass partition and gauze curtain are hazy and separate the bed and shower, bathing and bathing on both sides of the bathroom, there is also a cloakroom, office power *****, beverage refrigerator, coffee and tea small combination, electric lifting bed curtain, yoga mat and small dumbbells, B&O BeoPlay P2 A1 A2 portable wireless Bluetooth speakers and other facilities are still very good after so many years. The lobby on the first floor and the gym on the basement floor are great. I went to work out for half an hour. The swimming pool was very comfortable but unfortunately I didn't go in because I didn't bring my swimsuit. The noodle shop and the union bar and bar were all very nice;
2. Hygiene: The hygienic conditions are excellent. The combination of solid wood floors and furniture and white walls and glass window screens is very healing;
3. Environment: The Opposite House Hotel is located in the northern part of Sanlitun Commercial Street. I visited and studied during its construction in the early years. I had not graduated at that time. I came to visit and study again after graduation when the hotel opened. I was attracted by the glass curtain wall and the green grid behind it. It looked like an oasis in the city. But when I walked into the lobby, I found a sky-high atrium. The light and shadow in the room changed differently with different sunlight. There were art exhibitions, a strong humanistic and artistic cultural tone, and high-end stone and wood floors and the old solid wood door with metal nails at the entrance. It was very textured and had a strong contrast between the old and the new.
3. Service: I specifically asked the service staff to take me to the hotel guest room for a more systematic introduction. The service was really great, considerate, attentive and professional.
4. Maxi Guest Room Bar snacks and drinks: The welcome fruit plate and desserts on the table are great. The written notes give the guests staying in the hotel a feeling of being received at a friend's house, and also a feeling of "going home";
5. Finally, taking a bath in the bathtub and listening to the sound of water has a good healing effect. It also makes me realize what good products and good things are in this noisy era when hotels are overwhelmed by various new products emerging in an endless stream. Good standards and quality that will not fade with time are what should be done to make good things, good design + good materials + good construction + good quality + good details + good operation + good follow-up service + unique ultimate experience. Really good things must be used before you know it and you will never forget it!
